<IMG SRC="g152464dsp001.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">March&nbsp;16, 2021 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Dear Shareholders,
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">As an ExxonMobil investor, you face an important decision at this year&#146;s Annual Meeting of Shareholders on May&nbsp;26. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Engine No.&nbsp;1, a small, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">three-month-old</FONT> hedge fund with about an 0.02&nbsp;percent ownership in ExxonMobil, wants to make
big changes to our company. They have made false statements<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> about our plans and strategy. And they are proposing initiatives that would jeopardize our ability to generate the earnings and cash
flow that we need to pay our dividend, invest in future growth and work on technologies that will be important to help tackle climate change. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">We disagree with
their approach, and urge you to reject the four board candidates they&#146;ve nominated to carry out their value-destructive agenda. You can do that by voting the <B><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#82a9d9">BLUE PROXY CARD</FONT></B> to
support ExxonMobil&#146;s highly qualified and experienced Board of Directors and the multi-year strategy recently outlined to our investors. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Your Board and
management are fully committed to growing shareholder value by meeting the world&#146;s energy demands today and pursuing a technology-driven strategy to succeed through the energy transition. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Our investment portfolio is the best we&#146;ve had in over 20 years, and will grow earnings and cash flow, while remaining flexible to market conditions and benefiting
from ongoing cost-reduction efforts. Our strategy through 2025 will position ExxonMobil to emerge from the pandemic with improved financial performance and win in a lower-carbon energy future. Our plan: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt">Enables us to sustain and grow the dividend, </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt">Capitalizes on our industry-leading portfolio of resources to meet the world&#146;s demand for energy and deliver strong
cash-flow and returns, </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt">Positions the company as a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-cost</FONT> provider to compete effectively and maximize

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g152464dsp002.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Sustaining a Strong Dividend and Creating Long-Term Shareholder Value While Advancing the Transition to a
Lower-Carbon Future </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">ExxonMobil is committed to responsibly providing the energy that&#146;s needed today, and delivering shareholder value, while transitioning
to a lower-carbon future. Your Board and management have developed a strategy that is highly focused on that commitment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Engine No. 1&#146;s approach ignores the
role of oil and gas in the energy system of the future and the leadership role that ExxonMobil intends to play in reducing emissions through development and deployment of new lower-carbon technologies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Virtually all independent experts, including the United Nations Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change and the International Energy Agency, agree that oil and gas
will continue to be part of the world&#146;s energy mix for many years to come &#150; through 2050 and beyond even in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-carbon</FONT> scenarios. This is because it is well understood that oil and gas have unique
properties and benefits that, for some sectors of society, there are no current viable alternatives. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Without continuing near-term investment in oil and gas, the
world won&#146;t have enough energy to produce food, enable transportation and provide power to homes and industries that modernize communities and improve living standards around the world. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">As Microsoft founder Bill Gates says in his new book, &#147;How to Avoid a Climate Disaster,&#148; <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:14pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" ALIGN="center">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="100%"></TD></TR>


<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">
<TD VALIGN="top" BGCOLOR="#f0f1f2"> <P STYLE="font-size:8pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:2.00em; margin-right:2.00em; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#1055a0">&#147;Everyone deserves the chance to live a healthy and productive life &#150; and it&#146;s hard to stay
healthy if your local medical clinic can&#146;t keep vaccines cold because the refrigerators don&#146;t work. It&#146;s hard to be productive if you don&#146;t have lights to read by. And it&#146;s impossible to build an economy where everyone has
job opportunities if you don&#146;t have massive amounts of reliable, affordable electricity for offices, factories and call centers.&#148;</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-right:2.00em; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#e7261c"><B>BILL GATES</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:8pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt" align="left">&nbsp;</P></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">We congratulate Mr.&nbsp;Gates for his leadership on this issue and for illustrating the many facets of the challenge, that will require
multiple innovative solutions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">ExxonMobil will play a key role in helping advance these solutions. We are a technology company at our core and are focused on
understanding and advancing the fundamental science that will lead to the breakthroughs required to decarbonize the economy. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">That is why we are working on
solutions to help address the highest emitting sectors: manufacturing, commercial transportation and heavy industry, which account for 80&nbsp;percent of energy-related carbon emissions and where today&#146;s solutions are insufficient. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">With your Board&#146;s oversight and leadership, we are advancing and expanding our commitment to the development of
scalable, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-carbon</FONT> technologies for those key sectors, and plan $3&nbsp;billion in spending in this area through 2025. We recently announced the creation of ExxonMobil Low Carbon Solutions, a new business to
commercialize technologies from our extensive research and development portfolio built over the past decade. Projects under evaluation include: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:bottom">2</SUB> in the world. In addition to CCS, we are actively developing other lower emission technologies, such as hydrogen, advanced biofuels and new ways to reduce energy requirements of manufacturing.
These projects capitalize on our expertise and drive long-term shareholder value in markets that could be worth trillions of dollars in the decades ahead. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:14pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Over the past several years, your Board has successfully guided ExxonMobil through some of the most difficult conditions in the company&#146;s more than <FONT

dividend. </P>

transition. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">To illustrate, it&#146;s important for shareholders to know that ExxonMobil&#146;s planned investments in new projects will generate roughly
40&nbsp;percent of the company&#146;s operating cash flow in 2025. Engine No.&nbsp;1 has not said where cash flows needed to pay the dividend will come from if we elect their directors and adopt their
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ill-conceived</FONT> proposals. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">To put it bluntly, we have a plan that will grow earnings and cash flow, pay and grow the dividend,
fund future growth and position the company to have a meaningful role in the energy transition. Engine No.&nbsp;1 does not. They&#146;ve made false statements about our strategy. They don&#146;t have a plan. And their candidates for the Board do not
have the experience or knowledge to help lead your company through one of the most complex and challenging transitions the world has ever faced. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:14pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:48pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Cautionary Statement </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Outlooks; projections; goals; estimates; descriptions of strategic plans and objectives; planned capital and cash operating expense reductions and
the ability to meet or exceed announced reduction objectives; plans to reduce future emissions intensity and the expected resulting absolute emissions reductions; emission profiles of future developments; carbon capture results and the impact of
operational and technology efforts; future business markets like carbon capture or hydrogen; energy market evolution; product mix and sales growth; and other statements of future events or conditions in this letter are forward-looking statements.
Actual future results could differ materially due to a number of factors. These include global and regional changes in the demand, supply, prices, differentials or other market conditions affecting oil, gas, petroleum, petrochemicals and feedstocks;
company actions to protect the health and safety of employees, vendors, customers, and communities; the ability to access short- and long-term debt markets on a timely and affordable basis; the severity, length and ultimate impact of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> and government responses on people and economies; global population and economic growth; changes in law, taxes or regulation, including environmental regulations, taxes, political sanctions and
international treaties; the timely granting or freeze, suspension or revocation of government permits; the impact of fiscal and commercial terms and the outcome of commercial negotiations; feasibility and timing for regulatory approval of potential
investments or divestments; the actions of competitors and preferences of customers; the capture of efficiencies within and between business lines; unexpected technological developments; general economic conditions, including the occurrence and
duration of economic recessions; unforeseen technical or operating difficulties; the ability to bring new technologies to commercial scale on a cost-competitive basis, including large-scale hydraulic fracturing projects and carbon capture projects;
and other factors discussed here, in Item 1A. Risk Factors in our Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2020 and under the heading &#147;Factors Affecting Future Results&#148; on the Investors page of
our website at www.exxonmobil.com under the heading News&nbsp;&amp; Resources. For more information concerning the forward-looking statements, terms, and other information contained in this letter, please refer to the complete Analysts&#146; Meeting
presentation which is available live and in archive form through ExxonMobil&#146;s website at www.exxonmobil.com. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">ExxonMobil-operated
emissions, reductions and avoidance performance data are based on a combination of measured and estimated data using best available information. Calculations are based on industry standards and best practices, including guidance from the American
Petroleum Institute (API) and IPIECA. The uncertainty associated with the emissions, reductions and avoidance performance data depends on variation in the processes and operations, the availability of sufficient data, the quality of those data and
methodology used for measurement and estimation. Changes to the performance data may be reported as updated data and/or emission methodologies become available. ExxonMobil works with industry, including API and IPIECA, to improve emission factors
and methodologies. Emissions, reductions and avoidance estimates from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-ExxonMobil</FONT> operated facilities are included in the equity data and similarly may be updated as changes to the performance data are
reported. The data includes XTO Energy performance beginning in 2011. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Definitions and additional information concerning certain terms
used in this letter including cash operating expense are provided in the Frequently Used Terms available on the Investor page of our website at www.exxonmobil.com under the heading News&nbsp;&amp; Resources and in the March&nbsp;3, 2021
Analysts&#146; Day material referenced below. Reconciliations of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> terms are provided for historical periods but not for future periods. We are unable to provide a reconciliation of forward-looking <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> or other measures to the most comparable GAAP financial measures because the information needed to reconcile these measures is dependent on future events, many of which are outside management&#146;s control
as described above. Additionally, estimating such GAAP measures and providing a meaningful reconciliation consistent with our accounting policies for future periods is extremely difficult and requires a level of precision that is unavailable for
these future periods and cannot be accomplished without unreasonable effort. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures are estimated in a manner consistent with the relevant definitions and assumptions noted above.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The term &#147;project&#148; as used in this letter can refer to a variety of different activities and does not necessarily have the

Details concerning the nominees of ExxonMobil&#146;s Board of Directors for election at the 2021 Annual Meeting are included in the Proxy Statement. BEFORE MAKING ANY VOTING DECISION, INVESTORS AND SHAREHOLDERS OF THE COMPANY ARE URGED TO READ ALL

obtain a copy of the Proxy Statement and other relevant documents filed by ExxonMobil free of charge from the SEC&#146;s website, www.sec.gov. ExxonMobil&#146;s shareholders can also obtain, without charge, a copy of the Proxy Statement and other

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">End Notes: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">1.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Following are as examples of two false claims by Engine No.&nbsp;1. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Engine No.</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;1 Claim:</B> An Engine No.&nbsp;1 </FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>press release</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> on March&nbsp;3, 2021, critical of ExxonMobil&#146;s 2021 Investor Day presentation and describing a
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>white paper</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> issued by Engine No.&nbsp;1, said the following: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;This analysis [Engine No.&nbsp;1 white paper] details an evolving industry that requires significant long-term business model
innovation to enhance and protect shareholder value, <B>which contrasts sharply with the outlook set forth by ExxonMobil in its presentation to investors</B> today. &#133; About 2/3 of world greenhouse gas (GHG) emissions come from countries that
have net zero targets for emissions (mostly for 2050), and achieving those goals (or even coming close) will likely cause an implosion in fossil fuel demand, yet <B>ExxonMobil&#146;s presentation does not explore this widely-known range of possible
outcomes. </B>(Emphasis added)<B> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Fact:</B> ExxonMobil&#146;s </FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>2021 Investor Day presentation</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> showed a broad range of potential outcomes and discussed key technology requirements
of the future energy system. Future demand discussions were primarily based on scenarios from the UN Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change&#146;s Lower 2C scenarios from the
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>IPCC 2018 Special Report</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> (SR1.5) (on the impacts of global warming of 1.5&deg;C above <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-industrial</FONT> levels and related global greenhouse gas emission pathway), and included additional information from the </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>IPCC&#146;s Fifth
Assessment Report</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> (AR5). References to IPCC data can be found in ExxonMobil&#146;s 2021 </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>Investor Day
presentation</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> on pages 8, 9, 10, 14, 16, 18, 21, 59, 66, 68 and 69. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666"><B>Engine No 1 Claim:</B> In its March&nbsp;3 </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>white paper</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666">, Engine No.&nbsp;1 said the
following: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;What remains is a shrinking group of oil majors, notably ExxonMobil, that still <B>cling to old
forecasting methods and results.</B> At its annual investor day in March, 2020, which was held as the pandemic started gripping the world economy, <B>ExxonMobil painted a future unaware of how the world of policy was changing:</B> rising demand, a
big gap in necessary investment and a litany of concerns about mobilizing the investment needed to fill that gap.&#148; (Emphasis added) </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666"><B>Fact:</B> ExxonMobil&#146;s 2020 </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>Investor Day presentation</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> used data from the
respected International Energy Association&#146;s </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>Stated Policy Scenarios</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> (STEPS) and</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U> Sustainable Development Scenario</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> (SDS) which evaluate two very different policy environments. Per the IEA, STEPS
incorporates today&#146;s policy intentions and targets, while the SDS provides a strategic pathway to meet global climate, air quality and energy access goals in full. Even in the IEA SDS, which is a scenario that limits warming to less than 2
degrees Celsius, the IEA stated that $13 trillion in oil and gas investment is required over the next 20 years to meet demand. ExxonMobil&#146;s </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>Outlook for Energy</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> and </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>Energy and Carbon Summary</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> also highlight
the role of policy and technology in determining future demand. References to the IEA scenarios can be found in ExxonMobil&#146;s 2020 </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#1055a0"><U>Investor Day presentation</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" COLOR="#666666"> on pages 14, 20, 21, 22, 23 and 161. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
